CANDIDATE 1
generation_source: llm_primary (label: llm_primary)
raw_model_response: (not captured for this source)
extracted_sql:
SELECT SUM("sales_order_items"."line_subtotal") AS "total_shipped_gross_profit" FROM "sales_order_items" INNER JOIN "products" ON "sales_order_items"."product_id" = "products"."product_id" INNER JOIN "sales_orders" ON "sales_order_items"."order_id" = "sales_orders"."order_id" INNER JOIN "suppliers" ON "products"."supplier_id" = "suppliers"."supplier_id" INNER JOIN "warehouses" ON "sales_order_items"."warehouse_id" = "warehouses"."warehouse_id" WHERE "suppliers"."risk_level" = ? LAYER 9 — FINAL DECISION

selected_candidate_label: llm_sql_direct
selected_sql:
SELECT DISTINCT p.category
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE strftime('%Y', so.order_date) = '2025'
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi2
    JOIN sales_orders so2 ON soi2.order_id = so2.order_id
    WHERE soi2.product_id = p.product_id
    AND strftime('%Y', so2.order_date) = '2024'
)
